\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01167}01167 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)brief}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01168}01168 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> Return the Geometric distribution PDF values for a range of trials, starting at index `1`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01169}01169 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> If the probability of success on each trial is `successProb`, then the probability that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01170}01170 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> the `k`th trial (out of `k` trials) is the first success is `GeoLogPDF(k)`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01171}01171 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01172}01172 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]   successProb     :   The probability of success.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01173}01173 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]   logPdfPrecision :   The precision value below which the PDF is practically considered to be zero (**optional**).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01174}01174 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]   minSeqLen       :   The minimum length of the range of `k` values for which the PDF will be computed (**optional**).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01175}01175 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]   seqLen          :   The length of the range of `k` values for which the PDF will be computed (**optional**).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01176}01176 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !>                                  If provided, it will overwrite the the output sequence length as inferred from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01177}01177 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !>                                  the combination of `minSeqLen` and `logPdfPrecision`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01178}01178 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01179}01179 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01180}01180 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> `GeoLogPDF`  :   An allocatable representing the geometric PDF over a range of `k` values, whose length is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01181}01181 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !>                  `seqLen`, or if not provided, is determined from the values of `logPdfPrecision` and `minSeqLen`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01182}01182 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01183}01183 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)author}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01184}01184 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!    !> Amir Shahmoradi, Monday March 6, 2017, 3:22 pm, ICES, The University of Texas at Austin.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01197}01197 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        real(RK)                            :: logProbFailure}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01199}01199 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        logProbFailure = log(1.\_RK -\/ successProb)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01200}01200 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        if (present(seqLen)) then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01201}01201 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            lenGeoLogPDF = seqLen}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01202}01202 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        else}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01205}01205 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01206}01206 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!                lenGeoLogPDF = ceiling(LOG\_PDF\_PRECISION / logProbFailure)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01207}01207 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01208}01208 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            if (present(minSeqLen)) lenGeoLogPDF = max(minSeqLen,lenGeoLogPDF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01209}01209 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        end if}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01212}01212 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        do i = 2, lenGeoLogPDF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01213}01213 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!            GeoLogPDF(i) = GeoLogPDF(i-\/1) + logProbFailure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01214}01214 \textcolor{fortran_comment}{!        end do}}
